  3019. # [22:47] <@ehsan> right
  3020. # [22:48] <@ehsan> this all happens _before_ the instantiation
  3021. # [22:49] * mdas is now known as mdas|afk
  3022. # [22:49] <@ehsan> bz: I think perhaps the text froydnj linked to does a better job to describe this:
  3023. # [22:49] <@ehsan> "Now, back to our original problem. Why doesn’t the compiler look f up in the base class? First, notice that in the call to f() in the first code snippet, f is a non-dependent name. So it must be resolved at the point of the template’s definition. At that point, the compiler still doesn’t know what Base<T>::f is, because it can be specialized later. So it doesn’t look names up in the base class, but only in the enclosing
  3024. # [22:49] <@ehsan> scope. Since there’s no f in the enclosing scope, the compiler complains."
